 In a severe firefight in Tamil Nadu on Wednesday, 36 people died of burns while 50 others were injured
 nikatavarti mudhalipattee main ek pataakhaa factory parisar main lagi aag ne factory or parisar ke 48 shed ko tabah kar diya
 Police and fire sources said the accident occurred when factory workers were mixing chemicals to make colorful light-fired fireworks
 aag lagane se bahut se majdoor bheetar funs gaye
 The fire in the firecracker factory in this normally quiet village caused panic everywhere
 rah rahakar uthati dhamaakon kii aawaaj kareeb do kilometre ke daayre main sunai detii rahi
 The thick smoke spread over the area and the people trapped in the fire burnt so badly that it is difficult to even identify them
 haadase main hataahat hue logon main zyaadaatar factory main kaam karne vaale majdoor hai
 a tragic thing happened, police said, adding that some people who had entered the Om Shakti factory premises to save the people engulfed in the fire, also succumbed to the fire
 sutron ne bataaya ki sarkari paraamarsh kaa ulanghan karte hue saare pataakhon ko ek hi godaam main rakhaa gaya tha
 Fire brigade employees had to face a lot of difficulties due to lack of necessary items for relief work
 unke paas is tarah kii bheeshan aag ke khilaaf abhiyaan chalaane ke liye mask jaise jaruri upkarnon kaa abhaav tha
 They controlled the fire after four hours of hard work
 parisar ke ghaney dhuen main na ghus paane ke kaaran raahat or bachaav kaary prabhavit hua
 Labor department officials say the factory owner is absconding and did not heed the advice not to keep the stock of chemicals in one place
 pratyakshdarshiyon ne bataaya ki log dadhakati lapaton se ghire cheekh rahe the
 Relief workers rushed many injured to motorbikes, cots and shoulders
 adhikariyon ne bataaya ki factory main kaam karne vaale zyaadaatar majdoor akushal the or kuch pashchim bengal ke the, jinhen tamil bhashaa nahin aati thi, jisaki vajah se vah baaki logon ko aag lagane kii bare main bataa nahin paae
 Superintendent of Police of Virudhunagar district Najmul Hoda said that 90 percent of the total firecrackers made in the country are made in Sivakasi
 deepawali utsav sir par hone ke kaaran pataakhe banane kaa kaam yudhstar par chal rahaa tha
 a factory official said that 300 people were working in the unit at the time of the accident
 haadase ke baad factory ke baahar hajaaron log jamaa ho gaye, jo factory main kaam karne vaale apane sage sambandhiyon kii khayr khabar jaanane ke liye utsuk the
 Tamil Nadu Chief Minister Jayalalithaa announced a grant of Rs two lakh each to the kin of those who died and sent a team of five ministers to the spot to monitor the relief operations
 oktober 2009 main tiruvallur jile main pallipattu main pataakhon ke ek godaam main aag lagane se 32 logon kii maut ho gai thi
 Most of them went out to shop for Diwali
 varisht mantri o paneersevalam or unke chaar anya sahyogi raahat abhiyaanon par najar rakhane ke liye ghatnasthal par bheje gaye hai
 There are about 450 cracker factories in Sivakasi, where about 40,000 people work
 ek lakh se adhik log apratyaksh rup se isse jude hai or yahaan kaa vashirk kaarobaar 800 se 1000 karod rupee kaa he
 When the minister Paneesvalam and others reached the hospital to see the injured in Sivakasi, the family members of the victims surrounded them
 ye log aspataal main aparyaapt suvidhaon or dawaaon kii kami kii shikaayat kar rahe the
 Police said that in another incident, the foreman of the fire cracker unit was arrested in connection with the accident

 is notification kaa maqasad maveshi bazaar main jaanwaron kii kharid- bikri ko regulate karne ke saath maweshiyon ke khilaaf krurta rokna he

 BRICS - ye aathvaan bricks sammit he
 - It started in 2011
 - brazil, rus, bharat, china or dakshin africa iske sadsy hai
 - Its aim is to challenge the suzerainty of Western countries on the economic and political front
 - is summit main pradhanmantri narendra modi ke saath raashtrapati temer (brazil), raashtrapati putin (rus), raashtrapati shi jinnping (china) or raashtrapati zuma (dakshin africa) hissaa le rahe hai
 BIMSTEC (bay of Bengal Initiative for Technical and Economic Cooperation) - bimstek main bangladesh, bhutan, bharat, myanmar, nepal, srilanka or thailand shaamil hai
 - Five countries from South Asia and two from Southeast Asia (myanmar and Thailand)
 - bharat ne saarc deshon kii jagah bimstek deshon ko outrich meeting ke liye bulaayaa
 - This decision due to the emphasis on India's Act East Policy
 - pakistan main hone vaale saarc summit ke talane ke baad bimstek kii badi ahmiyat
 India will have these expectations
 
 
 - aatankwaad ke mudde par bricks or bimstek deshon kii taraf ekajute ninda kii ummid - BIMSTEC Countries - china or pakistan ke kootnithik rishton ke dekhte hue isamen mushkil ho saktaa he - Trying to revive BRICS organization in times of economic recession - aarthik morche par aapasi sahyog se mandi se ubarne ke upaay Bilateral visits - brazil, rus, bharat, china or dakshin africa ke saath dwipaksheeya mulaaqaatein China - china or rus ke saath dwipaksheeya baatcheet ahm
 - Talk to UN ban on Masood Azhar from China
 - seemapar aatankwaad ke mudde par saath dene ko lekar baat
 - Trying to get support from China on India's membership in NSG

 chipko andolan ke aaj 45 saal puure hone par search ingine google ne doodle banaakar yaad kiya he
 This movement started in Uttarakhand in 1974 to protect trees
 chipko andolan kii ek mukhya baat ye thi ki isamen mahilaon ne baari sankhya main bhaag liya tha
 As shown in the doodle, how women are trying to save them around trees like they did during the movement
 ye andolan uttarakhand se shuru hokar puure desh main fail gaya tha
 Let me tell you, in 1973, under the leadership of Gaura Devi, women clung to the trees to save them from cutting down trees
 is andolan ke madhyam se unhone wanon par apana paramparaagat adhikaar jataayaa tha
 This movement was widely given by environmentalists Sundarlal Bahuguna and Chandiprasad Bhatt
 yahaan lagaataar 9 ghante tak dikhaa indradhanush, bana vishwa recordjane andolan kii shuruuaat ke bare main
 
 
 On 26 March 1974, the 'chipko Movement' to stop felling of trees started
 us saal jab uttarakhand ke rani gaanv ke jangal ke lagbhag dhai hajaar pedo ko kaatane kii nilaamee hui, to gaura devi naam kii mahila ne anya mahilaon ke saath pedo kii nilaamee kaa virodh kiya
 Despite this, the decision of the government and the contractor did not change
 jab thekedaar ke aadmi ped kaatane pahunche, to gaura devi or unke 21 saathiyon ne un logon ko samajhane kii koshish kii
 When they insisted on cutting the trees, the women clung to the trees and challenged them to first cut us and then cut these trees
 ye hai duniya ke sabase chote 10 desh, 1 hajaar se kam he jansankhyamahilaon ke virodh ke aage thekedaar ko jhukna padaa
 Later, these women spoke before the officials of the local forest department
 jiske baad rani gaanv kaa jangal nahin kaata gaya
 Thus 'chipko Andolan' started here
 inaki vajah se shuru hua andolnavahin andolan ke dauraan paanchavin class tak padhi gaura devi kii paryaavaran vigyaan kii samaj or unki sooyeeboojh ne apane seene ko bandook ke aage kar ke, apni jaan par khel kar, jo kaam kiya, usne unhen sirf rani gaanv kaa hi nahin, uttarakhand kaa hi nahin, balki puure desh kaa hero bana diya tha
 She came to be called 'chipko Woman from India' abroad
 chipko andolan' ek adivasee aurat gaura devi ke adamya saahas or sooyeeboojh kii daastaan he
 This is the world's most expensive chocolate, the price was Rs 6 lakh after the movement
in Uttar Pradesh, this movement won a big victory in 1980 when the then Prime Minister Indira Gandhi stopped the felling of trees in the Himalayan forests of the state for 15 years
 Was applied
 baad ke saalon main yah andolan uttar main himachal pradesh, dakshin main karnataka, pashchim main rajasthan, purv main bihar or madhya bharat main failaa
 This movement was successful in stopping the felling of trees
